//--------------------------------------------------//
//-- New-Old Weapons Pack! - Weapon Sound Scripts --//
//--------------------------------------------------//
//
// Heya! This is a script file that I wouldn't recommend editing unless you want to change the Sound Scripts of one of my weapons for.. some reason.
// This file controls "Sound Scripts" - which Source games use as a proxy by which to call sounds if you want more control over them (also because they don't accept raw .wav files most of the time)
//
// If you want to add some new weapon sounds - perhaps for your own weapons, I'd recommend adding a new precache entry to the "game_sounds_manifest.txt" 
// That's all I have to say, thumb through this file if you want.
//
// Weapons are vaguely ordered in the order of implementation - for obvious reasons of me adding onto this file each time I add new stuff.
// There might be some scrapped stuff in here. It's whatever, I generally just leave them here on the off chance I return to them, even for funsies.
//
//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//

// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ //
// NOWP Legacy Stuff (Voice Lines)
// ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ //

// Channels
//	CHAN_AUTO		= 0,
//	CHAN_WEAPON		= 1,
//	CHAN_VOICE		= 2,
//	CHAN_ITEM		= 3,
//	CHAN_BODY		= 4,
//	CHAN_STREAM		= 5,		// allocate stream channel from the static or dynamic area
//	CHAN_STATIC		= 6,		// allocate channel from the static area 
// these can be set with "channel" "2" or "channel" "chan_voice"

//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// common attenuation values
//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

// DON'T USE THESE - USE SNDLVL_ INSTEAD!!!
//	ATTN_NONE		0.0f	
//	ATTN_NORM		0.8f
//	ATTN_IDLE		2.0f
//	ATTN_STATIC		1.25f 
//	ATTN_RICOCHET	1.5f
//	ATTN_GUNFIRE	0.27f

//	SNDLVL_NONE		= 0,
//	SNDLVL_25dB		= 25,
//	SNDLVL_30dB		= 30,
//	SNDLVL_35dB		= 35,
//	SNDLVL_40dB		= 40,
//	SNDLVL_45dB		= 45,
//	SNDLVL_50dB		= 50,	// 3.9
//	SNDLVL_55dB		= 55,	// 3.0
//	SNDLVL_IDLE		= 60,	// 2.0
//	SNDLVL_TALKING	= 60,	// 2.0
//	SNDLVL_60dB		= 60,	// 2.0
//	SNDLVL_65dB		= 65,	// 1.5
//	SNDLVL_STATIC	= 66,	// 1.25
//	SNDLVL_70dB		= 70,	// 1.0
//	SNDLVL_NORM		= 75,
//	SNDLVL_75dB		= 75,	// 0.8
//	SNDLVL_80dB		= 80,	// 0.7
//	SNDLVL_85dB		= 85,	// 0.6
//	SNDLVL_90dB		= 90,	// 0.5
//	SNDLVL_95dB		= 95,
//	SNDLVL_100dB	= 100,	// 0.4
//	SNDLVL_105dB	= 105,
//	SNDLVL_120dB	= 120,
//	SNDLVL_130dB	= 130,
//	SNDLVL_GUNFIRE	= 140,	// 0.27
//	SNDLVL_140dB	= 140,	// 0.2
//	SNDLVL_150dB	= 150,	// 0.2
